posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:I am very honored to be one of the first residents of the RV and experience the high-quality service of Nishi Haitai.

Facilities: Everything is new. It can be said that although the RV is not big, it has all the equipment you can think of. In addition to the necessary air conditioning, shower, TV and refrigerator, I was surprised when I was introduced to the sound and washing machine, and it was also equipped with beach chairs and egg roll tables. Later, I found that there was a sunshade roller blind, a small washing machine with air drying, and laundry detergent. The hardware facilities are absolutely great. The height of the washbasin is my favorite. If the child wets a piece of clothing, he can wash it easily without hurting his waist. The bed in the room is standard 1.5 meters, which is enough for the three of us, but the table can also be placed as a bed. The eldest child happily stayed on the dining table bed for one night. It is also equipped with children's slippers, children's bath towels and children's toothbrushes, which is very warm.

Hygiene: Brand new, very clean, no odor, sufficient water and electricity.

Environment: Nishi Haitai has a private beach, but the beach in front of the RV can definitely be regarded as its own beach. There is basically no one, and you can enjoy the sun, the beach and the waves alone. You can go to the sea when you go out, lie on the bed and watch the sunrise on the sea. The old mother can lie flat in the RV to watch the baby, and no baby will leave your sight.

Service: The service staff is very enthusiastic, and they will take the initiative to ask for help wherever they go. Help carry luggage, and respond quickly if there is a need. They also gave a double ticket to Yingzhiyu. The children are very happy.

Overall, I am very satisfied with this stay. My two children and I both give five-star praise, but there are a few points that can be improved, which can be used as a reference for the hotel and the children who come later.

First, about the network. We live in the farthest RV. TV needs wireless network to watch. I don‚Äôt know if there is a wifi signal in the nearby RV. The RV here does not have it. You need to connect to the mobile hotspot to watch it. We are on China Mobile‚Äôs network. Maybe the mobile phone signal is not very good, and watching TV will be a bit stuck. This can be improved.

It is better to provide a spare set of pillows and quilts. Two adults and one child stayed in, but there was only one double quilt and two pillows. The RV and the main building of the hotel may not have the same service system. The extra quilt was borrowed by the service staff from the main building of the hotel. Because the number of tourists was full during the May Day holiday, no extra pillows were borrowed. This is also a problem that the hotel can find a way to solve later.

RVs 1 to 11 on the beach are from the main building of the hotel, including restaurants and bathing centers. The closer the better, the more convenient, and the farther the better. I can run with two children, and the luggage is not heavy. No. 11 is very suitable for me üòÄ. If you bring the elderly and children, you can consider the distance.

Finally, the breakfast buffet in the restaurant is free for children under 1.2 meters, but the buffet dinner is free for children under 1.1 meters. Adult buffet dinner for guests staying in the hotel can be discounted by 20.

Yingzhitang Bath Single Ticket: The free hot spring ticket is very good. After a day of playing, you can go to the bubble to relieve fatigue. It is a child ticket for children over 1.1 meters, which is acceptable. Unfortunately, there is no parent-child shower room. The boy can swim and sweat steam, but he can't take a good bath.
